AN602 3.3.x Changelog

Skip

This is a non-exhaustive (but still near complete) changelog for AN602 3.3.x including release candidate versions. Our thanks to all those people who've contributed bug reports and code fixes.

Changes since 3.3.7

Bug

  • [AN602-13821] - Always show "Display this post" for foes

  • [AN602-16966] - "Insecure redirect" error while permanently deleting posts
  • [AN602-16976] - AN602 Native Search returns 1 match and one page of results
  • [AN602-16977] - Cron-job "img" tag at bottom breaks some styles and is inaccessible
  • [AN602-16978] - </ul> Tag Missing From posting_pm_header.html Template
  • [AN602-16981] - HTML-encoded emojis `&#128396;Ô∏è &#128208;` in email subject line
  • [AN602-16990] - Wrong style template code in the post editor prevents deleting a post with certain permission combination

Improvement

  • [AN602-13859] - Youtube profilefield needs an upgrade
  • [AN602-15947] - "X out of 0 messages stored" in UCP
  • [AN602-16800] - Language string NO_POSTS should be changed
  • [AN602-16959] - Remove redundant URL parameters from notification mails
  • [AN602-16967] - Deprecate use of PHP and INCLUDEPHP in templates
  • [AN602-16969] - Flash status displays when posting when posts settings don't allow [FLASH] - BBCode
  • [AN602-16988] - Ignore appended branch info when preparing commit message
  • [AN602-16991] - Add events for bookmarks and subscribed topics in UCP
